  Adds chapter on model equivalence and conversion

Introduces a new chapter detailing the equivalence

pseudocode, complexity analysis, and examples to ensure
a comprehensive understanding.

a comprehensive understanding.

  Adds chapter on model equivalence and conversion

a comprehensive understanding.

  Adds chapter on model equivalence and conversion

Introduces a new chapter detailing the equivalence
between deterministic and non-deterministic models.

elimination. The chapter includes formal definitions,
pseudocode, complexity analysis, and examples to ensure
a comprehensive understanding.
